\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
An \mbox{\hyperlink{classLepton_1_1Operation}{Operation}} represents a single step in the evaluation of an expression, such as a function, an operator, or a constant value. Each \mbox{\hyperlink{classLepton_1_1Operation}{Operation}} takes some number of values as arguments and produces a single value.

This is an abstract class with subclasses for specific operations.

Return an \mbox{\hyperlink{classLepton_1_1ExpressionTreeNode}{Expression\+Tree\+Node}} which represents the analytic derivative of this \mbox{\hyperlink{classLepton_1_1Operation}{Operation}} with respect to a variable.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em children} & the child nodes \\
\hline
{\em child\+Derivs} & the derivatives of the child nodes with respect to the variable \\
\hline
{\em variable} & the variable with respect to which the derivate should be taken \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{evaluate()}{evaluate()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [38/38]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual double Lepton\+::\+Operation\+::evaluate (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{double $\ast$}]{args,  }\item[{const std\+::map$<$ std\+::string, double $>$ \&}]{variables }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Perform the computation represented by this operation.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em args} & the array of arguments \\
\hline
{\em variables} & a map containing the values of all variables \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the result of performing the computation. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
